"Parametric" learning algorithm:
    Fit fixed set of parameters (θ ) to data.
"Non-parametric" learning algorithm:
    Amount of data/parameters you need to keep grows       (linearly) with size of data. May not be good if you have large amounts of data. ^VPh5cL3o
